\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00021}00021\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00022}00022\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ This\ header\ file\ does\ not\ require\ any\ macro\ definitions\ by\ the\ user}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00023}00023\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ (like\ CK\_DEFINE\_FUNCTION\ etc).\ \ In\ fact,\ it\ defines\ those\ macros}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00024}00024\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ for\ you\ (if\ useful,\ some\ are\ missing,\ let\ me\ know\ if\ you\ need}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00025}00025\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ more).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00026}00026\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00027}00027\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ There\ is\ an\ additional\ API\ available\ that\ does\ comply\ better\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00028}00028\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ GNU\ coding\ standard.\ \ It\ can\ be\ switched\ on\ by\ defining}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00029}00029\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ CRYPTOKI\_GNU\ before\ including\ this\ header\ file.\ \ For\ this,\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00030}00030\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ following\ changes\ are\ made\ to\ the\ specification:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00031}00031\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00032}00032\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ All\ structure\ types\ are\ changed\ to\ a\ "{}struct\ ck\_foo"{}\ where\ CK\_FOO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00033}00033\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ is\ the\ type\ name\ in\ PKCS\ \#11.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00034}00034\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00035}00035\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ All\ non-\/structure\ types\ are\ changed\ to\ ck\_foo\_t\ where\ CK\_FOO\ is\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00036}00036\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ lowercase\ version\ of\ the\ type\ name\ in\ PKCS\ \#11.\ \ The\ basic\ types}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00037}00037\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ (CK\_ULONG\ et\ al.)\ are\ removed\ without\ substitute.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00038}00038\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00039}00039\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ All\ members\ of\ structures\ are\ modified\ in\ the\ following\ way:\ Type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00040}00040\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ indication\ prefixes\ are\ removed,\ and\ underscore\ characters\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00041}00041\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ inserted\ before\ words.\ \ Then\ the\ result\ is\ lowercased.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00042}00042\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00043}00043\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ Note\ that\ function\ names\ are\ still\ in\ the\ original\ case,\ as\ they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00044}00044\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ need\ for\ ABI\ compatibility.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00045}00045\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pkcs11_8h_source_l00046}00046\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ CK\_FALSE,\ CK\_TRUE\ and\ NULL\_PTR\ are\ removed\ without\ substitute.\ \ Use}}
